Provider plan, availability, and speed tier data provided by <a href="https://www.broadbandnow.com/" rel="nofollow">BroadbandNow.com</a>. Speedtest real-world data is only present where sample size has reached significance within a region. Additionally, averages may include aggregated tests across multiple Internet Types (Fiber, DSL, Cable, etc.).</p></div></div></div></div></div><div class="section section-light section-sm section-bottom"><div class="container"><div class="pure-g"><div class="pure-u-1 u-c"><div class="u-full-width-text"><p>At Speedtest we pride ourselves on providing accurate and trustworthy data that forms the backbone of our ISP recommendations. Our real-world data is collected from millions of people worldwide who choose to take a Speedtest. This means our insights into ISP performance are reliable and current, allowing us to offer a clear, unbiased picture of ISP performance.</p><p>Three metrics will help you gauge the performance of an ISP: download speed, upload speed, and latency. Download speed is critical for tasks like streaming and downloading content, determining how swiftly data is transferred to your device. Upload speed is key for uploading content and engaging in online interactions, reflecting how quickly data is sent from your device to the internet. Latency, or ping, is essential in online gaming and video conferencing, influencing the responsiveness of your connection. With this comprehensive understanding of an ISP’s capabilities you have the data you need to&nbsp; make an informed choice based on your specific internet usage.</p><p>ISP technology plays an important role in determining the quality of your internet experience. Technologies like fiber optics typically offer the fastest speeds, making them ideal for high-demand online activities. Cable internet, a more widely available option, usually provides good download speeds but upload speeds may lag. DSL (digital subscriber line) offers moderate speeds sufficient for basic browsing and streaming. In contrast, satellite internet, often the only choice in remote locations, tends to have higher latency and slower speeds.</p></div></div></div></div></div><div class="section section-light"><div class="container"><div class="pure-g"><div class="pure-u-1 u-c"><p><img class="speed-needed-image pure-img" src="/s/images/speedtest/performance/image-speed-needs-1130px@1x.png" srcset="/s/images/speedtest/performance/image-speed-needs-1130px@2x.png 2x"></p></div><div class="pure-u-1 u-c"><h2>How Much Speed Do I Need?</h2><div class="u-full-width-text"><p>Download speeds of at least 100 Mbps and upload speeds of at least 10 Mbps are widely considered fast enough to handle nearly any online activity. A quick guide to what speeds you need for different online activities is below, and you can read our <a href="/about/knowledge/how-much-speed-you-need">full guide to internet speeds and performance</a> for more information. Keep in mind that the numbers below are the bare minimum for one device at a time. If you’re trying to use multiple devices on a network at the same time, you’ll want higher speeds.</p><div class="offer-speed-uses-container"><div class="offer-speed-ul-group u-c"><h3>0–5 Mbps (Slow)</h3><ul><li>Stream SD video</li><li>Connect on Slack</li><li>Use Microsoft Teams</li><li>Write and read email</li><li>Scroll social media</li><li>General web browsing</li></ul></div><div class="offer-speed-ul-group u-c"><h3>5–20 Mbps (Better)</h3><ul><li>Stream HD video at 1080p</li></ul></div><div class="offer-speed-ul-group u-c"><h3>20–40 Mbps (Solid)</h3><ul><li>Stream 4K video</li><li>Play games online</li></ul></div><div class="offer-speed-ul-group u-c"><h3>40–100 Mbps (Good)</h3><ul><li>Play HD games</li></ul></div><div class="offer-speed-ul-group u-c"><h3>100+ Mbps (Fast)</h3><ul><li>Engage in multi-player gaming</li><li>Download huge files</li></ul></div><div class="offer-speed-ul-group u-c"><h3>1+ Gbps (Very fast)</h3><ul><li>Do anything you want on multiple devices</li></ul></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="section section-light section-sm section-bottom-md"><div class="performance-content performance-content-type-fixed" id="fixed"><div class="section section-light section-sm section-bottom-md"><div class="container"><div class="pure-g"><div class="pure-u-1 u-c u-align-center"><h2>Sheridan Fixed Speeds</h2></div><div class="pure-u-1 u-c"><div class="panel"><div class="pure-g"><div class="pure-u-1 pure-u-md-1-3 u-c"><div class="performance-measure"><h3 class="performance-label"><svg class="svg-icon svg-icon-larger performance-icon-download"><use xlink:href="#ic_download"></use></svg>

  var $allControls = $('.performance-controls');
  initControls($allControls);

  // listen for toggle click
  $allControls.on('click', 'a[data-target]', function (e) {
    var $clicked = $(e.target).closest('a[data-target]');
    handleToggle($clicked);
    return false;
  });

  function moveDivider ($clicked) {
    var $divider = $clicked
      .closest('.performance-controls')
      .find('.performance-controls-divider');
    // move divider to correct position
    // control must be visible for outerWidth or position to work
    $divider.stop().fadeIn(0);
    $divider.css({
      'opacity': 1,
      'width': $clicked.outerWidth(),
      'left': $clicked.position().left,
    });
    // 150 matches @animation-speed in variables.less
    // delay slightly longer than that to prevent blinking
    $divider.stop().delay(200).fadeOut(0);
  }

  // do the work when the toggle is clicked
  function handleToggle ($clicked) {
    let nextToggle;
    if($clicked[0].innerHTML === "Mobile") {
      nextToggle = "fixed"
    } else if($clicked[0].innerHTML === "Fixed") {
      nextToggle = "mobile"
    } else if($clicked[0].innerHTML === "Download") {
      nextToggle = "upload"
    } else if($clicked[0].innerHTML === "Upload") {
      nextToggle = "download"
    }
    // set active class on button
    $clicked
      .closest('.performance-controls')
      .find('a[data-target]')
      .removeClass('active')
      .attr('aria-label', `Switch to ${nextToggle} speeds`)
      .attr('title', `Switch to ${nextToggle} speeds`)
    $clicked.addClass('active');
    $clicked.attr('aria-label', `Currently viewing ${$clicked[0].innerHTML.toLowerCase()} speeds`)
    $clicked.attr('title', `Currently viewing ${$clicked[0].innerHTML.toLowerCase()} speeds`)
    // fancy sliding animation
    moveDivider($clicked);
    // show/hide sections
    showTarget($clicked);
  }

  // toggle section according to data-target attribute
  function showTarget ($clicked) {
    $clicked
      .closest('.performance-controls')
      .find('a[data-target]')
      .each(function () {
        $($(this).data('target')).hide();
      });
    var $target = $($clicked.data('target'));
    $target.show();
  }

  // init each toggle control
  function initControls ($allControls) {
    // enable fancy styling
    $allControls.addClass('performance-controls-js');
    // make the first toggle in each group the active one
    // loop through these in reverse so no child controls are hidden the first time through
    // this allows the dividers to get the proper starting positions
    $($allControls.get().reverse()).each(function (i) {
      handleToggle($(this).find('a[data-target]').eq(0));
    });
  }
});

Internet"}}];

  function getProviderNames (data) {
    if(!data) { return }
    return data.map(function (provider) {
      var providerName = provider.provider_name;
      return providerName;
    })
  }

  function transformProviderData (data) {
    if(!data) { return }
    return data.filter((provider) => provider.p50_download_mbps && provider.p25_download_mbps && provider.p75_download_mbps)
      .map(function (provider, i) {
        var median = provider.p50_download_mbps;
        var low = parseInt(provider.p25_download_mbps);
        var high = parseInt(provider.p75_download_mbps);
        return { low, high, median };
      }
    );
  }

  function transformData (type, metric, data) {
    return data.map(function (month) {
      var date = new Date(month.period);
      var key = type + '_median_' + metric + '_mbps'
      return [ date.getTime(), month[key]];
    });
  }

  var marker = {
    symbol: 'circle',
    radius: 0.5,
  };

  var types = [];
  if (false) types.push('mobile');
  if (true) types.push('fixed');

  $.each(types, function (typeIndex, type) {
    var data = type === 'fixed' ? providerFixedData : providerMobileData;
    if (data) {
      var names = getProviderNames(data);
      var providerId = 'performance-graph-provider-' + type + '-' + 'download';
      var providerData = transformProviderData(data);
      var chartHeight = 415;
      if (providerData.length >= 10) {
        chartHeight = 700
      } else if (providerData.length >= 6) {
        chartHeight = 600;
      }
      //- For columnrange charts, position the tooltip at the median point instead of the center.
      //- This is done by wrapping the tooltip's updatePosition function to:
      //-   1) figure out which line is being hovered,
      //-   2) compute where that line's median would be in relation to the range of the chart,
      //-   3) override the tooltip's horizontal position with the median position.
      //- The first step above is definitely the most brittle. Getting the index of the currently
      //- hovered line is done by getting the desired position of the tooltip and comparing it to
      //- each line's "tooltip position" object. If they match, assume this is the correct line.
      //- It's brittle because if the values are overridden at any point (similar to what we are
      //- doing here), no match will be found. Maybe there's a more graceful way to find this
      //- index, but it seems to work ok. Once you have the index, you can access that line's
      //- data, and the rest is more straightforward.
      //- This functionality is "nice-to-have" and can be removed if it causes future problems.
      Highcharts.wrap(Highcharts.Tooltip.prototype, 'updatePosition', function() {
        //- first arg is callback, second arg is a point
        var args = Array.prototype.slice.call(arguments, 1);
        //- only do this for columnrange charts
        if (this.chart.types.length === 1 && this.chart.types[0] === 'columnrange') {
          //- we need the index of the hovered line so we can do math on the data
          //- we can infer the index by comparing the arg's plotY to the series data tooltipPos[1]
          var tooltipPos = this.chart.series[0].data.map(function (data) {
            return data.tooltipPos[1];
          });
          var index = tooltipPos.indexOf(args[0].plotY);
          //- only modify the tooltip position if the line positions match up
          if (index > -1) {
            var median = this.chart.series[0].data[index].median; // the provider's median
            //- make sure the median value exists
            if (median) {
              //- columnrange charts are inverted by default, so y is horizontal
              var yAxis = this.chart.yAxis[0]; // yAxis for the whole chart
              //- compute the ratio of median to series range
              var percent = (median - yAxis.min) / (yAxis.max - yAxis.min);
              //- plotX is usually the center of the range, but it's overwritten here
              //- tooltip position doesn't care if the chart is inverted
              args[0].plotX = yAxis.width * percent; // map ratio to pixels
            }
          }
        }
        arguments[0].apply(this, args); // proceed
      });

      // render provider chart
      Highcharts.chart(providerId, {
        title: {
          text: `Expected speed range (download)`,
        },
        xAxis: {
          categories: names,
          labels: {
            style: {
              color: 'white',
            },
          },
          accessibility: {
            rangeDescription: providerRangeLabels.x,
          },
        },
        tooltip: {
          positioner: function (width, height, point) {
            //- the point's plotX is modified by the updatePosition wrapper above
            return {
              x: this.chart.plotLeft + point.plotX - width / 2,
              y: this.chart.plotTop + point.plotY - height - 10,
            }
          },
          style: {
            color: 'white',
            fontSize: 12
          },
          padding: 4,
          headerFormat: '<p>Oct 2023 - Dec 2023</p><br/>',
          pointFormat: '<span style="color:{point.color}">\u25CF</span> {point.category}<br />Median Download: <b>{point.median}</b><br/>',
        },
        yAxis: {
          labels: {
            format: '{value:.0f}',
            step: 2,
          },
          softMin: 0,
          title: {
            text: 'Download (Mbps)',
            style: {
              color: 'white'
            }
          },
          accessibility: {
            rangeDescription: providerRangeLabels.y.download,
          },
        },
        chart: {
          styledMode: true,
          type: 'columnrange',
          inverted: true,
          marginBottom: 100,
          renderTo: providerId,
          //- (CT-5858) You must set the chart height or the chart will slowly get taller every time
          //- the viewport changes size, including when a mobile browser shows/hides chrome.
          height: chartHeight,
        },
        plotOptions: {
          series: {
            pointWidth: 3
          },
          columnrange: {
            colorByPoint: true,
            dataLabels: {
              enabled: false
            },
          }
        },
        credits: {
          enabled: false,
        },
        subtitle: {
          align: 'right',
          verticalAlign: 'bottom',
          floating: true,
          text: 'Oct 2023 - Dec 2023',
        },
        legend: {
          enabled: false,
        },
        series: [{
          name: names,
          data: providerData,
        }]
      });
    }

    $.each([ 'download', 'upload' ], function (metricIndex, metric) {
      var metricLabel = (metric === 'download') ? 'Download' : 'Upload';
      var id = 'performance-graph-historical-' + type + '-' + metric;
      var series = [];
      var lineChartColor = '#6afff3';
      var lineChartColorComparison = '#fff38e';
      if(metric === 'upload') {
        lineChartColor = '#bf71ff';
      }
      series.push({
        marker: marker,
        name: legendLabels.place[type][metric],
        data: transformData(type, metric, placeMonthlyData),
        color: lineChartColor
      });

      if (placeType === 'city' || placeType === 'postal-code') {
        series[0].color = lineChartColor;
        series.push({
          marker: marker,
          name: legendLabels.region[type][metric],
          data: transformData(type, metric, regionMonthlyData),
          color: '#fff38e'
        });
      }

      //Locations Chart
      Highcharts.chart(id, {
        title: {
          text: `Historical performance (${metric})`,
        },
        tooltip: {
          dateTimeLabelFormats: {
            day: '%b %Y'
          }
        },
        chart: {
          type: 'spline',
          styledMode: true,
          marginBottom: 100,
          renderTo: id,
          //- (CT-5858) You must set the chart height or the chart will slowly get taller every time
          //- the viewport changes size, including when a mobile browser shows/hides chrome.
          height: 415,
        },
        subtitle: {
          align: 'right',
          verticalAlign: 'bottom',
          floating: true,
          text: 'Jan 2023 - Jan 2024',
        },
        credits: {
          enabled: false,
        },
        xAxis: {
          type: 'datetime',
          labels: {
            format: '{value:%b}',
          },
          title: {
            text: undefined
          },
          accessibility: {
            rangeDescription: historicalRangeLabels.x,
          },
        },
        yAxis: {
          accessibility: {
            // escape single quotes since it's going in a js string
            rangeDescription: historicalRangeLabels.y[metric],
          },
          labels: {
            format: '{value:.2f}',
            step: 2,
          },
          softMin: 0,
          title: {
            text: undefined
          }
        },
        legend: {
          enabled: true,
          align: 'left',
          verticalAlign: 'bottom',
          floating: false,
          padding: 0,
          x: 50,
        },
        series: series
      });
    });
  });
});</script></body></html>
